 grih mantri amit shah ne kaha, 'yah pehali baar nahin he

 main aapke sabhi sanshayon ko dur karuunga

 China's Foreign Ministry spokeswoman Jiang Yu said he often spoke of retirement
 hamen lagata he ki ye antarrashtriya samudaay ko dhokhaa dene kii chaalen hai
 Two days before this, China called the Tibetan spiritual leader a wolf disguised as a Buddhist monk
 dalai lamas ne dharmashala main kaha tha ki vah tibeti nirvasit sarkaar ke raajnneetik pramukh ke taur par kaamkaaj chhod denge or aadhyatmik netaa bane rahenge
 He had said that he would continue to advocate meaningful autonomy for Tibet
 iske baad china kii taraf se kadi pratikriya ai
 Jiang said, the Dalai is a politically exiled leader in religious clothing
 vah tibeti nirvasiton kii gatividhiyon ke pramukh yojanakaar or raajnneetik sahyogi bhi hai
 On whether the Tibetan leader's decision to step down would affect negotiations between his colleagues and the Chinese government, he declined to answer, stating that Tibet's exiled government is an illegal political organization
 jiyang ne kaha, duniya kaa koi desh use manyata nahin detaa

 Wipro, India's third-largest IT service provider, is expected to reduce its workforce by about 47,000 in the next three years

 isisi ne haal hi main antarrashtriya maichon ke dauraan maidan par khadey nirnay kii samiksha karne vaali pranali shuru kii he

 5 fisadi kii vruddhi hui he
 The umpires gave a total of 72 decisions which is significantly higher than the DRS Test match average (49)
 match ke dauraan ampiron kii team ne nirnay dene main kul saat galat nirnay die, jinamein teen nirnyon ko thik nahin kiya gaya jabaki diares kii madad se chaar nirnay sudhaare gaye

 3, it increased to 95 after DRS was implemented

 andhra pradesh ke guntur ke kisaan appa raav ke paas jab koi chaara nahin bachaa to usne apni kidney bech di
 This 30 year old farmer kareeb ek saal pehle apni kidney bechi thi
 He was then told by the broker that four and a half lakh rupees would be given for the kidney
 appa ko dalal tamaam kagajaat dikhaae or bataaya ki puri prakriya kanoon ke tahat ho rahi he
 Those papers were signed by all government officials and doctors
 in puure kagajaton main yah kaha gaya ki appa raav ne apni kidney apni marji se paane vaale ke prati lagaav kii vajah se daan main di he
 After the completion of this process, Appa Rao was given only one third of the amount
 apni kidney ko 'bech' dene ke nirnay kaa kaaran bataate hue appa raav ne kaha ki 2009 main barish kii vajah se unki fasal puri tarah barabaad ho gai
 Appa then took money from a private businessman in the market at a higher interest for doing small business
 byaaj kii vajah se masik shulk bahut zyada ho gaya tha
 Appa could not refuse the offer to sell the kidney after this
 jab appa ne is bare main apane ghar main charchaa kii tab uski bivi or maa ne aisa kuch bhi karne manaa kar diya lekin maine kaha ki ab aatmahatya karne ke alaava koi or chaara bhi nahin rah gaya he
 Appa said, the broker cheated and did not pay more than two lakh rupees
 lekin main ab kisi se kuch kah bhi nahin saktaa
 Now my health has deteriorated
 kaam nahin kar saktaa
 i had to leave my village and hide my name
 bataa den ki andhra ke guntur main tamaam kisaan mirch or kapaas kii kheti karte hai
 Drought, storms and non-seasonal rains have destroyed their crops
 sthaneey logon ko appa raav kii kahani se zyada fark nahin padataa he
 All the farmers of Palanadu area also have the same story
 halaat ab yah ho gaye hai ki kuch ab khud hi dallali kaa kaam karne lage hai
 These case papers show that kidney removal surgery has been performed in large hospitals in Hyderabad and following the entire legal process
 tamaam kidney bechney vaale apana naam tak bataane ko raji nahin hote hai
 They feel that by doing so, they themselves will be caught in legal trouble
 tippaniyan The senior police officer says that there will be no benefit even by taking action in these cases because everything depends on the papers in the court
 abhi tak in maamalon main ek bhi cese darj nahin kiya gaya he
 The State Human Rights Commission has now written to the government to investigate the matter thoroughly and report on the actual situation
 ayog ne poocha he ki aakhir kaise is tarah maanav angon ke pratyrpan kaa gaiyr-kanoonee kaam chal rahaa he
 The report is expected to arrive by the end of April
